  • The deepfakes technology made a great gift to the world: freedom from manipulation by the media. Knowledge about deepfakes will make people question everything they read, hear and see on TV, in the press and online. Very soon, each time people will read, hear or see anything they will think: "it might be fake: if they can even generate fake videos of people saying fake things on camera, why would I believe the words I read or the voice I hear?" Thanks to deepfakes, without proofs, everything, independently of who is the medium, is just a rumor. Without proofs, no one is wrong, no one is right. It's just your opinion against mine. It's so liberating.
